When I went swimming as a hotel guest at 10 o'clock in the morning, I was told by the pool staff that there was a training class for children learning to swim. There were many people, so try to come at noon. But I checked out at noon and left to catch the train, so I couldn't swim at noon. I was about to sign and wanted to make do with swimming. A middle-aged male staff member came over and said to me as a hotel guest: "There are students in the training class. There are too many people. You insist on going swimming now. What should I do?"
The swimming pool that hotel guests can use for free cannot be used because the hotel outsources it to a third-party training class in order to make extra money. It is also accused of being inconsiderate. This is too much!
Afterwards, although the hotel staff came to apologize and wanted to compensate and be forgiven, I did not accept or need any financial compensation. I just hoped that the hotel would improve. This kind of ** practice of neglecting service in order to make money should not happen. The hotel gave me an umbrella when I checked out. Although I accepted the other party's humility, I still firmly refused to accept the hotel's mistake unless it could be proven that the improvements would not affect subsequent guests!

Because I had to catch the high-speed train the next morning, I didn't want to stay in an express hotel, and I wanted to be closer to the high-speed rail station. The price wasn't too expensive, so I chose this place after a quick comparison. I feel like I made the right choice, very satisfied!
The first thing I feel is the service staff at the front desk. They are very enthusiastic. I booked a room in a non-main building. Because the price is cheap, I thought the arrangement would be very biased. But when we arrived, the front desk took the initiative to upgrade our room in the main building for free, which made us feel good when we first arrived in a different place!
The second room is very clean and tidy and feels warmer.
Third, the breakfast is rich and has many varieties.
Fourth, it is really close to the high-speed rail station. There are about two or three traffic lights. Because I was worried about not being able to make it in time, I took a taxi. It only took three or four minutes to get to the station. If I know this next time, I can save money on taxis.
Unfortunately, I checked in late and rushed early, so I didnâ€™t think about taking photos.
Here are some real experiences for your reference.
